################################
#####     PRISON        ################
################################
//transforms a dwarf into a "imprisoned dwarf". You can chose different lenghts of stay.
//needs 1meat for each month, and 1drink for each 3months. 
//imprisoned dwarf is immobile, blind, mute, has only 10% strength, toughness and agility.
//For each month in prison, the dwarf will permanently lose 2% strength, toughness and agility. Prison is tough.
//example: 10 months: 10 meat, 4 drinks. Dwarf will lose 20% of his strength, toughness and agility.

[REACTION:SKILL_PRISON_DWARF][NAME:========ANY SKILL========][BUILDING:PRISON:NONE]

[REACTION:PRISON_1_MONTH]
[NAME:Imprison a dwarf for 1 month]
[BUILDING:PRISON:CUSTOM_A]
 [REAGENT:drink1:150:DRINK:NONE:NONE:NONE]            
   [REAGENT:drink container1:1:NONE:NONE:NONE:NONE]
      [CONTAINS:drink1][PRESERVE_REAGENT]
[REAGENT:E:1:MEAT:NONE:NONE:MUSCLE][DOES_NOT_DETERMINE_PRODUCT_AMOUNT]
[PRODUCT:100:1:BOULDER:NONE:INORGANIC:PRISON_1_MONTH]
[PRODUCT:0:1:BOULDER:NONE:INORGANIC:ANNOUNCEMENT_PRISON]
